// https://github.com/ytdl-org/youtube-dl/blob/master/youtube_dl/extractor/nbc.py

notes:
 * only queries metadata for a single video
 * shows how to structure a query,
   rather than referencing a saved query by its hash (as is done by the website)

// https://stackoverflow.com/questions/42021113/how-to-use-curl-to-access-the-github-graphql-api
// https://stackoverflow.com/a/51895358

query='query bonanzaPage(
    $app: NBCUBrands! = nbc
    $name: String!
    $oneApp: Boolean
    $platform: SupportedPlatforms! = web
    $type: EntityPageType! = VIDEO
    $userId: String!
  ) {
    bonanzaPage(
      app: $app
      name: $name
      oneApp: $oneApp
      platform: $platform
      type: $type
      userId: $userId
    ) {
      data {
        sections {
          ... on LinksSelectableGroup {
            data {
              items {
                ... on Shelf {
                  data {
                    items {
                      ... on VideoTile {
                        data {
                          locked
                          programmingType
                          permalink
                          mpxGuid
                          seasonNumber
                          episodeNumber
                          airDate
                          duration
                          title
                          secondaryTitle
                          longDescription
                        }
                      }
                    }
                  }
                }
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }'

query="$(echo $query)"

curl 'https://friendship.nbc.co/v2/graphql' \
  --insecure \
  -H 'content-type: application/json' \
  -H 'accept: application/json' \
  -X POST \
  --data-binary '{"query":"'"$query"'","variables":{"app":"nbc","name":"chicago-pd","oneApp":true,"platform":"web","type":"TITLE_V2","userId":"0"}}'

query='query bonanzaPage(
    $app: NBCUBrands! = nbc
    $name: String!
    $seasonNumber: Int
    $oneApp: Boolean
    $platform: SupportedPlatforms! = web
    $type: EntityPageType! = VIDEO
    $userId: String!
  ) {
    bonanzaPage(
      app: $app
      name: $name
      seasonNumber: $seasonNumber
      oneApp: $oneApp
      platform: $platform
      type: $type
      userId: $userId
    ) {
      data {
        sections {
          ... on LinksSelectableGroup {
            data {
              items {
                ... on Stack {
                  data {
                    items {
                      ... on VideoTile {
                        data {
                          locked
                          programmingType
                          permalink
                          mpxAccountId
                          mpxGuid
                          seasonNumber
                          episodeNumber
                          airDate
                          duration
                          title
                          secondaryTitle
                          longDescription
                        }
                      }
                    }
                  }
                }
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }'

query='query bonanzaPage(
    $app: NBCUBrands! = nbc
    $name: String!
    $seasonNumber: Int
    $oneApp: Boolean
    $platform: SupportedPlatforms! = web
    $type: EntityPageType! = VIDEO
    $userId: String!
  ) {
    bonanzaPage(
      app: $app
      name: $name
      seasonNumber: $seasonNumber
      oneApp: $oneApp
      platform: $platform
      type: $type
      userId: $userId
    ) {
      data {
        sections {
          ... on LinksSelectableGroup {
            data {
              items {
                ... on Stack {
                  data {
                    items {
                      ... on VideoTile {
                        data {
                          locked
                          programmingType
                          permalink
                          mpxAccountId
                          mpxGuid
                          seasonNumber
                          episodeNumber
                          airDate
                          duration
                          title
                          secondaryTitle
                          longDescription
                        }
                      }
                    }
                  }
                }
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }'

query="$(echo $query)"

curl 'https://friendship.nbc.co/v2/graphql' \
  --insecure \
  -H 'content-type: application/json' \
  -H 'accept: application/json' \
  -X POST \
  --data-binary '{"query":"'"$query"'","variables":{"app":"nbc","name":"chicago-pd","oneApp":true,"platform":"web","type":"TITLE_V2_EPISODES","userId":"0"}}'
